 The Rupani cabinet decided that now farmers will be provided 10 hours of electricity
 vijay rupani sarkaar kaa bada faisladansal abtak gujarat main 8 ghanta bijli mili thi, jise badhaakar ab 10 ghanta kiya gaya he, pichley dinon gujarat main kaaphi kam barish hui he, jis vajah se kisaanon ke liye ye faisla liya gaya ki unhen ab 2 ghanta zyadabizli muhaiyakarwaai jaaegi, taaki wo apane fasalon ko sinchai ke jariye pani pahunchaa paae or kisaanon kaa nuksaan naa ho
 It is considered to extend electricity from 8 hours to 10 hours, after providing 24 hours single phase electricity under Jyotigram Yojana after Narendra Modi became Chief Minister in the villages of Gujarat
 modi sarkaar se pehle 4 ghante tak bijli milti thi
